<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модель.html>моде́ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">modɛ́lʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:моделировать.html>модели́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">modɛlírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:моделировать.html>модели́ровать</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смоделировать.html>смодели́ровать</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">art</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to model, to sculpture</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:модернизированный.html>модернизи́рованный</a></b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <ol><li>—</li>
<li>частичн.: <a href = vnd.unilang:современный.html>совреме́нный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:стильный.html>сти́льный</a></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модуль.html>мо́дуль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">módulʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модуль.html>мо́дуля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модуль.html>мо́дули</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модуль.html>мо́дулей</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мо́дульный</b>)

***можно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a> (103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мог-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mog-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (but the form **<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мо́жный</span> does not exist).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мочь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">močʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The forms "**<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">немо́жно</span>" or "**<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a></span>" are not used in standard Russian. To negate <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a></span>, use <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nelʹzjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which doesn't have a positive form "<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">льзя</span>", or <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможно.html>возмо́жно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ne vozmóžno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>мо́ж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a></b>
</p><p>Предикатив; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-можно-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***мозг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозг</a> (970)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mozgъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mozg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мо́зга</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозги́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозго́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> brain; marrow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головной.html>головно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">golovnój mozg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cerebrum</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спинной.html>спинно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мо́зг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">spinnój mózg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">spinal cord</span></div></dd>

***мой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> (55)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mojь</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мойка.html>мо́йка</a> (13962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мойка.html>мо́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mójka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мойка.html>мо́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мойка.html>мо́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мойка.html>мо́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>washing</li>
<li>sink (basin), kitchen sink</li>
<li>washer</li></ol>

***мокнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мокнуть.html>мо́кнуть</a> (15242)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мокнути</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">moknuti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*moknǫti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to become/get wet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокнуть.html>мо́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">móknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to get wet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мокнуть.html>мо́кнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>móknutʹ</b> pod doždjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be out in the rain</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to soak</li></ol>

***мол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мол.html>мол</a> (933)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">môle</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мол.html>мол</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mol</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мол.html>мо́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мол.html>мо́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мол.html>мо́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>jetty, mole, breakwater, pier <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">protective structure to protect areas from sea waves</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молвить.html>мо́лвить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mólvitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to say</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мол.html>мол</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mol</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> he says, they say <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">used informally to mark reported speech</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́т</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мол.html>мол</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On mne govorít, <b>mol</b>, daváj dénʹgi!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He says to me, <b>he says</b>, "give me the money!"</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:молва.html>молва́</a> (18068)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мълва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mŭlva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mъlva</i>; cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">млъва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mlŭva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">noise, mourning</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">мо́ва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">móva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">language</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">мо́ва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">móva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">language</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">mowa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">language</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">мълва́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mǎlvá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rumour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">mluva</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молва.html>молва́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">molvá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молва.html>молвы́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>rumour/rumor, talk, hearsay
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1849</b>,  Fyodor Dostoyevsky,  <cite>Netochka Nezvanova</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почти.html>почти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всюду.html>всю́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:носиться.html>носи́лась</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:молва.html>молва́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неограниченный.html>неограни́ченном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:честолюбие.html>честолю́бии</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Počtí vsjúdu nosílasʹ <b>molvá</b> o jevó neograníčennom čestoljúbii.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Almost everywhere floated the <b>rumor</b> of his unbounded ambition.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
